msg:The first stop of the return trip after the holiday, I stayed at the Guangzhou Emerald Hilton. It is located in Huangpu District. The location is relatively remote but the environment is very good. The hotel looks a little old. Because I had to go on the next day, I chose this Hilton, which is relatively close to the expressway. Because of the "pet-friendly" nature of this trip, the "Hilton" brand has doubled its favorability. Especially this one, they made a pet-friendly space manual and drew the cub walking route in the hotel, which is really considerate.
[Pet-friendly] Although the pet-friendly room can only be a twin room without a balcony on the second floor, the hotel has done a good job in details. The pet room is also well furnished. The room has no view at all, the 2nd floor is flush with the trail, the sound of raindrops hitting the ground is relatively loud on rainy days, the windows are not soundproof, walking outside, the sound of pushing carts is basically immersive. For dogs who love to bark when they walk around strangely, the location of the pet room is actually unreasonable. Fortunately, my young master has long been used to living in hotels, he is completely indifferent to the sound, and sleeps like a pig on the dog bed by himself.
[Pet cleaning fee] 300r
[Pet check-in procedure] You need to show the vaccine certificate, and the lady at the front desk will take a photo.
[Environment] The hotel as a whole looks a little old, and the natural environment is very good. If it is not raining, it is absolutely amazing to go for a jog in the morning!
[Service] Absolutely praise, whether it is the concierge, the front desk, the breakfast room waiter, the manager or the hotel staff you meet, the service awareness is very good! When I was a little confused and didn't know where to go, if there were staff nearby, they would definitely come and ask me where I wanted to go and if there was anything I needed to help. Confidence, enthusiasm, and professional attitude doubled my favorability for this hotel, and I feel very warm.
[Breakfast] There are not many varieties, but they are definitely delicious. Today's small bug: the recommended pork ribs are not cooked enough, and they are very hard. Small surprise: the freshly baked garlic buns are really delicious! The collision of salty and sweet taste buds opened up the little beauty of the morning! I was amazed, it would be even better if it was not so oily
[Room] The pet room has twin beds. The bedding is very comfortable and soft. The room has a good sense of space, and the twin beds don't feel cramped. The shower equipment is a bit old and doesn't quite fit the hotel's positioning. The sanitation of the room needs to be improved, especially the glue left by the previous guests on the toilet.
The overall sense is that it is a pet-friendly hotel worth living in. The next time I pass by Guangzhou, I will choose this place again if I bring my dogüëè
Small suggestion: It would be even more perfect if you can open more pet rooms with different floors and room types! üòÑ
(Personally, I think "pet-friendly" is a two-way street. When businesses open their arms to this group, they hope that pet owners can raise dogs in a civilized way. In particular, it is recommended to take good care of fur children and do not go to the toilet at will indoors, and clean them up in time when they go to the toilet outdoors. )

The gym has a wide view and is transparent, and the children's amu*****t facilities near the restaurant are very eye-catching. Although it can meet my personal needs (coffee, porridge, rice noodles), it is still slightly inadequate compared to other five stars. Maybe the hotel has been around for a long time, and if it can be refurbished, it will definitely attract more customers.
